                    <div class="listingDescription_1woxt0o" data-reactid="997">
                     <div data-reactid="998">
                      <div data-reactid="999">
                       This house is a large Craftsman home, an LA classic built in 1909! This bedroom for guests faces the large back yard and has two big windows, and light colored real wood floors, real bed, desk with office chair. Very centrally located, close to downtown LA and USC, 10 and 110 Fwys. Large backyard with fruit trees and patio furniture to enjoy the sunny LA weather. Free parking right in front of the house; equipped with washer, dryer and dishwasher.
                      </div>
                      <div data-reactid="1000">
                       This is a classic four bedroom LA Craftsman home shared with the host, co-host, Marley the Bosnian cat, Jack the small American dog, and potentially another Airbnb guest. It has housed people from all over the world for over a decade, both for long term and short stays (more reviews on CS as VONVON). There is ample free street parking. Large back yard with lemon, avocado and apple trees, and big front yard. The house is big, 1600 sq ft, with large living room that includes flatscreen with Hulu and Netflix, dining room with large table and spacious fully equipped kitchen - so no feeling cramped. The bedroom is small but cozy, sleeps one in a comfy twin size bed. It has a desk/vanity and chair, two mirrors, and a rack to hang clothes with hangers provided. It has light colored real wood floors, two big windows overlooking the large back yard, a night stand, clean towels, blow dryer and snacks. Help yourself to tea and coffee in the kitchen. For those who may have mobility issues, the house is a single story but there are 4 steps up to the porch and also down into the back yard.
                      </div>
                      <div data-reactid="1001">
                       This is the 'hood you have heard about in rap songs. Is it scary? Naaah - come check it out for yourself. We are on a nice family street shared with an elementary school (ice cream trucks are the bonus amenity!) The neighborhood has just been proposed to be officially declared by the LA City Planning Department a "Los Angeles Character Neighborhood" ('cause we have character!) A film crew favorite.... Very close to the museum complex - California Science Center, Natural History Museum, African American Museum - and also to University of Southern California, the LA Coliseum and LA Sports Arena. Staples Center/LA Live and the LA Convention Center is an 8 dollar Uber ride away (parking there for 3 hrs costs $25!) Very centrally located and easy freeway and public transit access so you can visit all major LA sites including the beach without spending hours in traffic. Please read the neighborhood description including pics provided by airbnb by the map. If this is not the location you had in mind, please search for Beverly Hills, Hollywood, Santa Monica or whatever other city you are really interested in. Los Angeles is a huge place so if it's your first time to visit, do searches of distances between sights in the greater Los Angeles area to get a realistic idea of how much time you will need to get around to really see all you want to see, especially if you will be using public transport only. You might want to consider staying for a shorter time in different areas or renting a car to get around like most Angelinos. We want guests who are happy to come to our vibrant neighborhood and are realistic in their expectations of Los Angeles. Thank you!

                      <div data-reactid="1206">
                       Looking for an Affordable, Clean, Comfortable, and Efficient Private 2br Cottage for your visit to Los Angeles. This is a private little house, which has EVERYTHING you need for your home away from home. 833 sq ft 2 bedrooms Living room Dining room Kitchen 1 baths BEDROOMS- can comfortably sleep 4 people. 1 bedroom has queen size bed 1 bedroom has a Full size bed. Comfortably sleeps up to 4 and is perfect for both, small families or couples. 1 Single Air mattress with liens is provided for your convenience. Hotel quality fresh linens for each bed will be provided. There are plenty of pillows, blankets, Towels, and closets in each bedroom for storage. BATHROOM - 1 full bathroom completely tiled shower/tub STYLE- This is a Traditional, chic and updated home. You will feel like you are staying in a peaceful Hideaway. Come enjoy our beautiful oasis in the City. This Cottage will be your peaceful hideaway in vibrate Los Angeles. There is an abundance of natural light and cool ocean breezes, because there are 2 windows in every room. Both bedrooms have Lined Roman Shades in every window to darken it for privacy or for sleeping in. The Cottage has a back yard with fresh fruit and Vegetables in the Garden, a patio with a barbecue grill, and water fountain features in the garden The Kitchen is fully equipped with modern appliances, Fridge, Range w/ Microwave, Dishwasher, coffee maker; and toaster oven, dishes etc. This Cottage is fully air conditioned and heated with a Central heating and Air Conditioning system for your comfort. (No window unit! No hot or cold spots!) PARKING: Parking is always premium in Los Angeles. The cottage has access to plenty of parking. Off Street parking in the driveway accommodates 4 cars and 2 parking spaces are available on the street in front of the house. Parking is never a problem. The street parking rules are posted in the house manual. EXTRAS- Wifi Access to Hi-speed Internet; and Directv Service The house is professionally cleaned before your arrival. $250 deposit required which is refunded after your stay. $100 Cleaning fee. Check-in is 3pm Check-out is 11am Depending on other bookings we are flexible on check-in times. AVAILABILITY The Calendar is UP TO DATE if it shows available; it's available so feel free to Instant book! You may instant book 7 days in advance. Home is available for filming for an additional fee, please contact us for details. Extended stays of 3 weeks or More Weekly Housekeeping services included. A 14% City Tax is required All Major Credit Cards accepted

                       An exciting adventure awaits at the Cimarron House, home of L.A.’s best shared housing. We are family owned and operated. In this home away from home, you’ll have access to daily free hot breakfast, convenient public transportation, freeway access, free high speed Internet and laundry.                       <div data-reactid="1329">
                       The house is attached to a historic Hollywood mansion, originally built by iconic African-American actor Eddie "Rochester" Anderson. There is a furnished kitchen and dining area, living room, free laundry machines, and a large backyard with swimming pool and outdoor tables. Free wifi is available throughout the property.
                      </div>
                      <div data-reactid="1330">
                       In mid-city Los Angeles, a mere ten minutes from USC, our properties are centrally located in the heart of the city (6 miles from Hollywood and Downtown LA, 12 miles from the beach.) The closest Metro stop is a 10-minute walk, and will take you directly to Santa Monica, downtown, and other popular tourist destinations. We are just 3 miles from Culver City, with its many dining options, parks and hiking trails, farmer's markets, and galleries.

                      <div data-reactid="1453">
                       Right smack dab in the middle of the major attractions and only 5 miles from The Los Angeles International Airport (LAX). Midway between Disneyland and Hollywood. Midway between Knotts Berry Farm and Universal Studios. Midway between downtown Los Angeles and the best beaches that Southern California has to offer. We are five minutes from Larry Flints '2' gambling casinos - Lucky Lady and the Hustler. We are 5-minutes walking distance from a supermarket, a variety store, restaurants and a movie theater. We are five minutes away from two rental car businesses. We are 10 minutes from LAX on a good day. (5 miles away on any day). Two minutes walking distance from public transportation that will take you anywhere, literally. I am currently a top rated professional rideshare driver with two major companies and former chauffeur/tour guide although the wife takes "tour guiding" to a higher level. The wife and I own this cozy little house in a clean, quiet, middle-class neighborhood. Our house has been owned by our family since it was purchased new, in 1946. The wife and I have lived in it, ourselves, since 2003. We are fortunate in many respects. First of all, we have the best neighborhood you could imagine. We love our neighbors. They're the the best in the West. We exchange Christmas and birthday gifts with them. Our neighbors are all super friendly to our AIRbnb guests. They all are families who have been homeowners in the neighborhood for an average of 27 years. One could not ask for better neighbors! Please, be respectful of them as they surly will of you. Give ‘em a friendly smile and a wave. Let them know you are friendly, as well. If you are driving, please try to park directly in front of our house. Out of respect, our neighbors usually try to leave a space open for our guests - if at all possible. If you cannot find a space directly in front of our house, just give me a call and I will move my car around back and you can have my space. You should not have to rent a car but if you are bringing a car to park at our house please note the following weekly street-sweeping parking restriction: Do not park across our street (on the opposite side) on Mondays between the hours of 10 AM and 1 PM as posted on the warning signs on the street. Do not park on our side of the street between the hours of 10 AM and 1 PM Tuesdays as posted on the warning signs. Sometimes the warning signs are not nearby. The citation is just shy of $50. One more parking concern, if you're on our house side of the street your car must not face against the other cars but must park heading in the same, in other words just notice the Direction that the other cars are facing and do not park the opposite direction of the other cars on the same side of the street. It is assumed that newcomers know the laws. There are no signs warning about which way your car should face when parked. Probably the next best thing about our location is the climate in this particular section (The Gardena Valley) of Los Angeles county. It is cooler in the summertime, than most of the rest of the Los Angeles area.                       <div data-reactid="1710">
                       In the heart of Los angeles, lies the forever changing gem, Mid-City. Upon arriving you will notice the blend of cultures that live here. You can find all kinds of food, drinks, places to see and experiences to be had. You will enjoy LA here!
                      </div>
                      <div data-reactid="1711">
                       The exposed brick wall really sets the industrial ambiance. New york style apartment meets a bohemian mid century artist when you first open the door. You will find a freshly cleaned bed with mood lighting upon entering. To the right you'll find the fully equipped kitchen with coffee and coffee maker. A clean, practical desk sits next to the right window and to the left of the kitchen, perfect for work during your stay. The unit has a standing shower, equipped with a full range of water temperatures. Hot showers when you need them! The bathroom has everything you would need for daily hygiene. The parking is on the street and is usually very easy. Make sure to read the street signs before you park. If you have any questions, please feel free to reach out to me. I am here to make your stay comfortable, clean, easy and enjoyable.
                      </div>
                      <div data-reactid="1712">
                       Gentrified and cultured, Mid-City is close to everything in Los Angeles. You are 15-20 minutes driving distance to: - Santa Monica - West hollywood - Koreatown - Staples center - Downtown - Griffith Park - LACMA - Venice Beach - Hollywood - Inglewood -Culver City -Marina Del Ray - Convention center You can enjoy: - Hiking - Surfing - Bike riding - Music - Movies - Entertainment - Restaurants You are really close to the 10 highway. Giving you quick access to the open road.
